Check if WordPress credentials file already exists\n   267→    WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE=\"$HOME_DIR/.wordpress_${DOMAIN_NAME}_credentials\"\n   268→\n   269→    if [[ -f \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" ]]; then\n   270→        print_info \"WordPress credentials file already exists\"\n   271→        print_step \"Reading existing credentials...\"\n   272→        DB_NAME=$(grep \"^DB_NAME=\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" | cut -d'=' -f2)\n   273→        DB_USER=$(grep \"^DB_USER=\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" | cut -d'=' -f2)\n   274→        DB_PASSWORD=$(grep \"^DB_PASSWORD=\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" | cut -d'=' -f2)\n   275→        WP_ADMIN_USER=$(grep \"^WP_ADMIN_USER=\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" | cut -d'=' -f2)\n   276→        WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD=$(grep \"^WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD=\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" | cut -d'=' -f2)\n   277→        WP_ADMIN_EMAIL=$(grep \"^WP_ADMIN_EMAIL=\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" | cut -d'=' -f2)\n   278→        print_success \"Using existing WordPress configuration\"\n   279→    else\n   280→        print_step \"Generating secure passwords...\"\n   281→        DB_PASSWORD=$(generate_password)\n   282→        WP_ADMIN_USER=\"admin\"\n   283→        WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD=$(generate_password)\n   284→        WP_ADMIN_EMAIL=\"admin@$DOMAIN_NAME\"\n   285→\n   286→        # Check if we can access MySQL without password\n   287→        # This is needed when MySQL root user has password authentication enabled\n   288→        MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN=\"\"\n   289→        MYSQL_ACCESS_RESTORED=false\n   290→\n   291→        print_step \"Checking MySQL root access...\"\n   292→        if mysql -u root -e \"SELECT 1\" > /dev/null 2>&1; then\n   293→            print_success \"MySQL root access available\"\n   294→        else\n   295→            # MySQL root has password authentication enabled\n   296→            # Temporarily switch to auth_socket to allow access without password\n   297→            print_warning \"MySQL root password is enabled. Temporarily enabling passwordless access...\"\n   298→\n   299→            # Get current authentication plugin for root user\n   300→            # We need to use mysqld --skip-grant-tables to access the database\n   301→            print_step \"Stopping MySQL service...\"\n   302→            systemctl stop mysql\n   303→\n   304→            # Ensure the socket directory exists (required for mysqld_safe)\n   305→            print_step \"Ensuring MySQL socket directory exists...\"\n   306→            mkdir -p /var/run/mysqld\n   307→            chown mysql:mysql /var/run/mysqld\n   308→            chmod 755 /var/run/mysqld\n   309→\n   310→            print_step \"Starting MySQL in recovery mode...\"\n   311→            # Start MySQL without grant tables (allows access without password)\n   312→            mysqld_safe --skip-grant-tables --skip-networking &\n   313→            MYSQLD_PID=$!\n   314→            sleep 3\n   315→\n   316→            # Get the current authentication plugin\n   317→            MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN=$(mysql -u root -N -e \"SELECT plugin FROM mysql.user WHERE user='root' AND host='localhost';\" 2>/dev/null || echo \"\")\n   318→\n   319→            if [[ -z \"$MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN\" ]]; then\n   320→                MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN=\"caching_sha2_password\"\n   321→            fi\n   322→\n   323→            print_info \"Current root authentication plugin: $MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN\"\n   324→\n   325→            # Switch root to auth_socket temporarily\n   326→            print_step \"Switching root to auth_socket authentication...\"\n   327→            mysql -u root -e \"UPDATE mysql.user SET plugin='auth_socket' WHERE user='root' AND host='localhost';\"\n   328→            mysql -u root -e \"FLUSH PRIVILEGES;\"\n   329→\n   330→            # Stop mysqld_safe\n   331→            print_step \"Restarting MySQL in normal mode...\"\n   332→            kill $MYSQLD_PID 2>/dev/null || true\n   333→            sleep 2\n   334→            # Make sure all MySQL processes are stopped\n   335→            pkill -9 mysqld 2>/dev/null || true\n   336→            sleep 1\n   337→\n   338→            # Start MySQL normally\n   339→            systemctl start mysql\n   340→            sleep 2\n   341→\n   342→            # Verify we can now connect\n   343→            if mysql -u root -e \"SELECT 1\" > /dev/null 2>&1; then\n   365→            print_info \"Database user '$DB_USER' already exists\"\n   366→            print_warning \"Existing database user password will NOT be changed to protect existing applications.\"\n   367→            print_info \"If this WordPress installation cannot connect to the database,\"\n   368→            print_info \"please manually update the password or provide existing credentials.\"\n   369→            # Note: We don't change the password here to avoid breaking existing applications\n   370→            # that may be using this user. The administrator should provide existing credentials\n   371→            # in the wp-config.php file or credentials file.\n   372→        else\n   373→            print_step \"Creating database user '$DB_USER'...\"\n   374→            mysql -e \"CREATE USER '$DB_USER'@'localhost' IDENTIFIED BY '$DB_PASSWORD';\"\n   375→            print_success \"Database user created\"\n   376→        fi\n   377→\n   378→        print_step \"Granting privileges...\"\n   379→        mysql -e \"GRANT ALL PRIVILEGES ON $DB_NAME.* TO '$DB_USER'@'localhost';\"\n   380→        mysql -e \"FLUSH PRIVILEGES;\"\n   381→        print_success \"Database privileges granted\"\n   382→\n   383→        # Restore original root authentication plugin if we changed it\n   384→        if [[ \"$MYSQL_ACCESS_RESTORED\" == \"true\" ]] && [[ -n \"$MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN\" ]]; then\n   385→            print_step \"Restoring original root authentication ($MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN)...\"\n   386→            mysql -e \"UPDATE mysql.user SET plugin='$MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN' WHERE user='root' AND host='localhost';\"\n   387→            mysql -e \"FLUSH PRIVILEGES;\"\n   388→            print_success \"MySQL root authentication restored\"\n   389→        fi\n   390→\n   391→        print_step \"Saving WordPress credentials...\"\n   392→        cat > \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" << EOF\n   393→DB_NAME=$DB_NAME\n   394→DB_USER=$DB_USER\n   395→DB_PASSWORD=$DB_PASSWORD\n   396→WP_ADMIN_USER=$WP_ADMIN_USER\n   397→WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD=$WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD\n   398→WP_ADMIN_EMAIL=$WP_ADMIN_EMAIL\n   399→EOF\n   400→ 403→    fi\n   404→\n   405→    # Export for later use\n   406→    export DB_NAME DB_USER DB_PASSWORD WP_ADMIN_USER WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD WP_ADMIN_EMAIL\n   407→}\n   408→\n   409→download_wordpress() {\n 571→setup_wordpress_site() {\n   572→    print_header \"Setting Up WordPress Site\"\n   573→\n   574→    # Check if WordPress is already installed (tables exist)\n   575→    print_step \"Checking if WordPress is already installed...\"\n   576→\n   577→    # Run wp-cli as www-data user from the WordPress directory\n   578→    # This is required because PHP 8.3+ uses posix_spawn which fails if the\n   579→    # current working directory is not accessible to the target user (www-data).\n   580→    # By using 'cd $INSTALL_DIR && ...' we ensure the CWD is accessible.\n   581→    if sudo -u www-data bash -c \"cd '$INSTALL_DIR' && '$WP_CLI_PATH' core is-installed --path='$INSTALL_DIR'\" 2>/dev/null; then\n   582→        print_info \"WordPress is already installed\"\n   583→        print_step \"Skipping WordPress setup...\"\n   584→        print_success \"Using existing WordPress installation\"\n   585→        return\n   586→    fi\n   587→\n   588→    print_step \"Running --url='https://$DOMAIN_NAME' \\\n   592→        --title='$SITE_TITLE' \\\n   593→        --admin_user='$WP_ADMIN_USER' \\\n   594→        --admin_password='$WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD' \\\n   595→ '$INSTALL_DIR' && '$WP_CLI_PATH' option update time_format 'H:i' --path='$INSTALL_DIR'\"\n   608→    print_success \"WordPress settings updated\"\n   609→}\n   610→\n   611→optimize_php_fpm() {\n   612→    print_header \"Optimizing PHP-FPM Configuration\"\n   613→\n   614→    local PHP_VERSION\n   615→    PHP_VERSION=$(php -r \"echo PHP_MAJOR_VERSION.'.'.PHP_MINOR_VERSION;\")\n   616→    local PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF=\"/etc/php/${PHP_VERSION}/fpm/pool.d/www.conf\"\n   617→    local PHP_INI_CONF=\"/etc/php/${PHP_VERSION}/fpm/conf.d/30-wordpress-overrides.ini\"\n   618→\n   619→    # Calculate optimal number of PHP processes based on available memory\n   620→    print_step \"Calculating optimal PHP process settings...\"\n   621→\n   622→    local PHP_MEM_LIMIT\n   623→    local AVAIL_MEM\n   624→    local MAX_PHP_PROCESSES\n   625→\n   626→    # Get PHP memory limit (default 128M if not set)\n   627→    PHP_MEM_LIMIT=$(php -r \"echo ini_get('memory_limit');\" 2>/dev/null || echo \"128M\")\n   628→    # Convert to bytes\n   629→    PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=$(echo \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT\" | numfmt --from=iec 2>/dev/null || echo \"134217728\")\n   630→\n   631→    # Get available memory in bytes\n   632→    AVAIL_MEM=$(grep MemAvailable /proc/meminfo | awk '{print $2}')\n   633→    AVAIL_MEM_BYTES=$((AVAIL_MEM * 1024))\n   634→\n   635→    # Calculate max processes: available memory / PHP memory limit, with minimum of 5\n   636→    MAX_PHP_PROCESSES=$(echo \"${AVAIL_MEM_BYTES}/${PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES}+5\" | bc 2>/dev/null || echo \"10\")\n   637→\n   638→    # Cap at reasonable maximum\n   639→    if [[ \"$MAX_PHP_PROCESSES\" -gt 50 ]]; then\n   640→        MAX_PHP_PROCESSES=50\n   641→    fi\n   642→\n   643→    print_info \"Available memory: $((AVAIL_MEM / 1024)) MB\"\n   644→    print_info \"PHP memory limit: $PHP_MEM_LIMIT\"\n   645→    print_info \"Calculated max PHP processes: $MAX_PHP_PROCESSES\"\n   646→    print_info \"Note: You may want to tune this value for your specific workload (typically 10-100)\"\n   647→\n   648→    # Create PHP configuration overrides\n   649→    if [[ ! -f \"$PHP_INI_CONF\" ]]; then\n   650→        print_step \"Creating PHP configuration overrides...\"\n   651→        cat > \"$PHP_INI_CONF\" << PHPCONF\n   652→; WordPress-specific PHP overrides\n   653→; Generated by WordPress installer\n   654→\n   655→; Set a larger maximum upload size\n   656→upload_max_filesize=${UPLOAD_MAX_FILESIZE}\n   657→post_max_size=${UPLOAD_MAX_FILESIZE}\n   658→\n   659→; Write error log to syslog for easier debugging\n   660→error_log=syslog\n   661→\n   662→; Performance optimizations\n   663→opcache.enable=1\n   664→opcache.memory_consumption=128\n   665→opcache.interned_strings_buffer=8\n   666→opcache.max_accelerated_files=10000\n   667→opcache.revalidate_freq=2\n   668→opcache.save_comments=1\n   669→PHPCONF\n   670→        print_success \"PHP configuration overrides created\"\n   671→    else\n   672→        print_info \"PHP configuration overrides already exist\"\n   673→    fi\n   674→\n   675→    # Update PHP-FPM pool configuration for dynamic process management\n   676→    if [[ -f \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\" ]]; then\n   677→        print_step \"Updating PHP-FPM pool configuration...\"\n   678→\n   679→        # Backup original config\n   680→        if [[ ! -f \"${PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF}.original\" ]]; then\n   681→            cp \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\" \"${PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF}.original\"\n   682→        fi\n   683→\n   684→        # Update pm settings for dynamic process management\n   685→        sed -i \"s/^pm = .*/pm = dynamic/\" \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\"\n   686→        sed -i \"s/^pm.max_children = .*/pm.max_children = ${MAX_PHP_PROCESSES}/\" \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\"\n   687→        sed -i \"s/^pm.start_servers = .*/pm.start_servers = 5/\" \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\"\n   688→        sed -i \"s/^pm.min_spare_servers = .*/pm.min_spare_servers = 2/\" \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\"\n   689→        sed -i \"s/^pm.max_spare_servers = .*/pm.max_spare_servers = 10/\" \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\"\n   690→\n   691→        # Restart PHP-FPM to apply changes\n Set up variables for the installer user\n    CURRENT_USER=\"$INSTALLER_USER\"\n    HOME_DIR=$(eval echo ~$INSTALLER_USER)\n    INSTALL_DIR=\"/var/www/$DOMAIN_NAME\"\n\n    print_success \"Installer user configured: $INSTALLER_USER\"\n    print_info \"Home directory: $HOME_DIR\"\n    print_info \"Installation directory: $INSTALL_DIR\"\n}\n\ncheck_ubuntu() {\n    if ! grep -q \"Ubuntu\" /etc/os-release 2>/dev/null; then\n        print_warning \"This script is designed for Ubuntu. Proceed with caution on other distributions.\"\n    fi\n}\n\n#-------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Main installation functions\n#-------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nshow_banner() {\n    clear\n    echo \"\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   +-------------------------------------------------------------------------+${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   |${NC}                                                                         ${CYAN}|${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   |${NC}   ${BOLD}${WHITE}WordPress${NC}                                                            ${CYAN}|${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   |${NC}   ${MAGENTA}Automated Installation Script for Ubuntu 24.04${NC}                       ${CYAN}|${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   |${NC}                                                                         ${CYAN}|${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   |${NC}   ${WHITE}This script will install and configure:${NC}                              ${CYAN}|${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   |${NC}   ${GREEN}*${NC} WordPress CMS (latest version)                                     ${CYAN}|${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   |${NC}   ${GREEN}*${NC} MySQL Database Server                                              ${CYAN}|${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   |${NC}   ${GREEN}*${NC} Nginx Web Server                                                   ${CYAN}|${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   |${NC}   ${GREEN}*${NC} PHP with required extensions                                       ${CYAN}|${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   |${NC}   ${GREEN}*${NC} SSL certificate via Let's Encrypt                                  ${CYAN}|${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   |${NC}                                                                         ${CYAN}|${NC}\"\n    echo -e \"${CYAN}   +-------------------------------------------------------------------------+${NC}\"\n    echo \"\"\n}\n\nparse_arguments() {\n    # Database name derived from domain (replace dots and dashes with underscores)\n    DB_NAME=\"wp_$(echo \"$DOMAIN_NAME\" | tr '.-' '_' | cut -c1-16)\"\n    DB_USER=\"wp_$(echo \"$DOMAIN_NAME\" | tr '.-' '_' | cut -c1-10)\"\n\n    # Check if WordPress credentials file already exists\n    WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE=\"$HOME_DIR/.wordpress_${DOMAIN_NAME}_credentials\"\n\n    if [[ -f \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" ]]; then\n        print_info \"WordPress credentials file already exists\"\n        print_step \"Reading existing credentials...\"\n        DB_NAME=$(grep \"^DB_NAME=\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" | cut -d'=' -f2)\n        DB_USER=$(grep \"^DB_USER=\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" | cut -d'=' -f2)\n        DB_PASSWORD=$(grep \"^DB_PASSWORD=\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" | cut -d'=' -f2)\n        WP_ADMIN_USER=$(grep \"^WP_ADMIN_USER=\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" | cut -d'=' -f2)\n        WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD=$(grep \"^WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD=\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" | cut -d'=' -f2)\n        WP_ADMIN_EMAIL=$(grep \"^WP_ADMIN_EMAIL=\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" | cut -d'=' -f2)\n        print_success \"Using existing WordPress configuration\"\n    else\n        print_step \"Generating secure passwords...\"\n        DB_PASSWORD=$(generate_password)\n        WP_ADMIN_USER=\"admin\"\n        WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD=$(generate_password)\n        WP_ADMIN_EMAIL=\"admin@$DOMAIN_NAME\"\n\n        # Check if we can access MySQL without password\n        # This is needed when MySQL root user has password authentication enabled\n        MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN=\"\"\n        MYSQL_ACCESS_RESTORED=false\n\n        print_step \"Checking MySQL root access...\"\n        if mysql -u root -e \"SELECT 1\" > /dev/null 2>&1; then\n            print_success \"MySQL root access available\"\n        else\n            # MySQL root has password authentication enabled\n            # Temporarily switch to auth_socket to allow access without password\n            print_warning \"MySQL root password is enabled. Temporarily enabling passwordless access...\"\n\n            # Get current authentication plugin for root user\n            # We need to use mysqld --skip-grant-tables to access the database\n            print_step \"Stopping MySQL service...\"\n            systemctl stop mysql\n\n            # Ensure the socket directory exists (required for mysqld_safe)\n            print_step \"Ensuring MySQL socket directory exists...\"\n            mkdir -p /var/run/mysqld\n            chown mysql:mysql /var/run/mysqld\n            chmod 755 /var/run/mysqld\n\n            print_step \"Starting MySQL in recovery mode...\"\n            # Start MySQL without grant tables (allows access without password)\n            mysqld_safe --skip-grant-tables --skip-networking &\n            MYSQLD_PID=$!\n            sleep 3\n\n            # Get the current authentication plugin\n            MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN=$(mysql -u root -N -e \"SELECT plugin FROM mysql.user WHERE user='root' AND host='localhost';\" 2>/dev/null || echo \"\")\n\n            if [[ -z \"$MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN\" ]]; then\n                MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN=\"caching_sha2_password\"\n            fi\n\n            print_info \"Current root authentication plugin: $MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN\"\n\n            # Switch root to auth_socket temporarily\n            print_step \"Switching root to auth_socket authentication...\"\n            mysql -u root -e \"UPDATE mysql.user SET plugin='auth_socket' WHERE user='root' AND host='localhost';\"\n            mysql -u root -e \"FLUSH PRIVILEGES;\"\n\n            # Stop mysqld_safe\n            print_step \"Restarting MySQL in normal mode...\"\n            kill $MYSQLD_PID 2>/dev/null || true\n            sleep 2\n            # Make sure all MySQL processes are stopped\n            pkill -9 mysqld 2>/dev/null || true\n            sleep 1\n\n            # Start MySQL normally\n            systemctl start mysql\n            sleep 2\n\n            # Verify we can now connect\n            if mysql -u root -e \"SELECT 1\" > /dev/null 2>&1; then\n                print_success \"MySQL root access temporarily enabled\"\n                MYSQL_ACCESS_RESTORED=true\n            else\n                print_error \"Failed to enable MySQL root access\"\n                print_info \"Please check MySQL configuration and try again\"\n                exit 1\n            fi\n        fi\n\n        print_step \"Checking if database '$DB_NAME' exists...\"\n        if mysql -e \"USE $DB_NAME\" 2>/dev/null; then\n            print_info \"Database '$DB_NAME' already exists\"\n        else\n            print_step \"Creating database '$DB_NAME'...\"\n            mysql -e \"CREATE DATABASE $DB_NAME DEFAULT CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci;\"\n            print_success \"Database created\"\n        fi\n\n        print_step \"Checking if database user '$DB_USER' exists...\"\n        USER_EXISTS=$(mysql -sse \"SELECT EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM mysql.user WHERE user = '$DB_USER' AND host = 'localhost');\")\n        if [[ \"$USER_EXISTS\" == \"1\" ]]; then\n            print_info \"Database user '$DB_USER' already exists\"\n            print_warning \"Existing database user password will NOT be changed to protect existing applications.\"\n            print_info \"If this WordPress installation cannot connect to the database,\"\n            print_info \"please manually update the password or provide existing credentials.\"\n            # Note: We don't change the password here to avoid breaking existing applications\n            # that may be using this user. The administrator should provide existing credentials\n            # in the wp-config.php file or credentials file.\n        else\n            print_step \"Creating database user '$DB_USER'...\"\n            mysql -e \"CREATE USER '$DB_USER'@'localhost' IDENTIFIED BY '$DB_PASSWORD';\"\n            print_success \"Database user created\"\n        fi\n\n        print_step \"Granting privileges...\"\n        mysql -e \"GRANT ALL PRIVILEGES ON $DB_NAME.* TO '$DB_USER'@'localhost';\"\n        mysql -e \"FLUSH PRIVILEGES;\"\n        print_success \"Database privileges granted\"\n\n        # Restore original root authentication plugin if we changed it\n        if [[ \"$MYSQL_ACCESS_RESTORED\" == \"true\" ]] && [[ -n \"$MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN\" ]]; then\n            print_step \"Restoring original root authentication ($MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN)...\"\n            mysql -e \"UPDATE mysql.user SET plugin='$MYSQL_ROOT_AUTH_PLUGIN' WHERE user='root' AND host='localhost';\"\n            mysql -e \"FLUSH PRIVILEGES;\"\n            print_success \"MySQL root authentication restored\"\n        fi\n\n        print_step \"Saving WordPress credentials...\"\n        cat > \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\" << EOF\nDB_NAME=$DB_NAME\nDB_USER=$DB_USER\nDB_PASSWORD=$DB_PASSWORD\nWP_ADMIN_USER=$WP_ADMIN_USER\nWP_ADMIN_PASSWORD=$WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD\nWP_ADMIN_EMAIL=$WP_ADMIN_EMAIL\nEOF\n        chown \"$CURRENT_USER\":\"$CURRENT_USER\" \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\"\n        chmod 600 \"$WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\"\n        print_success \"Credentials saved to $WP_CREDENTIALS_FILE\"\n    fi\n\n    # Export for later use\n    export DB_NAME DB_USER DB_PASSWORD WP_ADMIN_USER WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD WP_ADMIN_EMAIL\n}\n\ndownload_wordpress() {\n    print_header \"Installing WordPress\"\n\n    if [[ -d  print_header \"Installing WP-CLI\"\n\n    WP_CLI_PATH=\"/usr/local/bin/wp\"\n\n    if [[ -f \"$WP_CLI_PATH\" ]]; then\n        print_info \"WP-CLI already installed\"\n        print_step \"Updating WordPress Site\"\n\n    # Check if WordPress is already installed (tables exist)\n    print_step \"Checking if WordPress is already installed...\"\n\n    # Run wp-cli as www-data user from the WordPress directory\n    # This is required because PHP 8.3+ uses posix_spawn which fails if the\n    # current working directory is not accessible to the target user (www-data).\n    # By using 'cd $INSTALL_DIR && ...' we ensure the CWD is accessible.\n    if sudo -u www-data bash -c \"cd '$INSTALL_DIR' && '$WP_CLI_PATH' core is-installed --path='$INSTALL_DIR'\" 2>/dev/null; then\n        print_info \"WordPress is already installed\"\n        print_step \"Skipping WordPress setup...\"\n        print_success \"Using existing WordPress installation\"\n        return\n    fi\n\n    print_step \"Running WordPress installation...\"\n    sudo -u www-data bash -c \"cd '$INSTALL_DIR' && '$WP_CLI_PATH' core install \\\n        --path='$INSTALL_DIR' \\\n        --url='https://$DOMAIN_NAME' \\\n        --title='$SITE_TITLE' \\\n        --admin_user='$WP_ADMIN_USER' \\\n        --admin_password='$WP_ADMIN_PASSWORD' \\\n        --admin_email='$WP_ADMIN_EMAIL' \\\n        --skip-email\"\n\n    print_success \"WordPress installation completed\"\n\n    print_step \"Setting permalink structure...\"\n    sudo -u www-data bash -c \"cd '$INSTALL_DIR' && updated\"\n}\n\noptimize_php_fpm() {\n    print_header \"Optimizing PHP-FPM Configuration\"\n\n    local PHP_VERSION\n    PHP_VERSION=$(php -r \"echo PHP_MAJOR_VERSION.'.'.PHP_MINOR_VERSION;\")\n    local PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF=\"/etc/php/${PHP_VERSION}/fpm/pool.d/www.conf\"\n    local PHP_INI_CONF=\"/etc/php/${PHP_VERSION}/fpm/conf.d/30-wordpress-overrides.ini\"\n\n    # Calculate optimal number of PHP processes based on available memory\n    print_step \"Calculating optimal PHP process settings...\"\n\n    local PHP_MEM_LIMIT\n    local AVAIL_MEM\n    local MAX_PHP_PROCESSES\n\n    # Get PHP memory limit (default 128M if not set)\n    PHP_MEM_LIMIT=$(php -r \"echo ini_get('memory_limit');\" 2>/dev/null || echo \"128M\")\n    # Convert to bytes\n    PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=$(echo \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT\" | numfmt --from=iec 2>/dev/null || echo \"134217728\")\n\n    # Get available memory in bytes\n    AVAIL_MEM=$(grep MemAvailable /proc/meminfo | awk '{print $2}')\n    AVAIL_MEM_BYTES=$((AVAIL_MEM * 1024))\n\n    # Calculate max processes: available memory / PHP memory limit, with minimum of 5\n    MAX_PHP_PROCESSES=$(echo \"${AVAIL_MEM_BYTES}/${PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES}+5\" | bc 2>/dev/null || echo \"10\")\n\n    # Cap at reasonable maximum\n    if [[ \"$MAX_PHP_PROCESSES\" -gt 50 ]]; then\n        MAX_PHP_PROCESSES=50\n    fi\n\n    print_info \"Available memory: $((AVAIL_MEM / 1024)) MB\"\n    print_info \"PHP memory limit: $PHP_MEM_LIMIT\"\n    print_info \"Calculated max PHP processes: $MAX_PHP_PROCESSES\"\n    print_info \"Note: You may want to tune this value for your specific workload (typically 10-100)\"\n\n    # Create PHP configuration overrides\n    if [[ ! -f \"$PHP_INI_CONF\" ]]; then\n        print_step \"Creating PHP configuration overrides...\"\n        cat > \"$PHP_INI_CONF\" << PHPCONF\n; WordPress-specific PHP overrides\n; Generated by WordPress installer\n\n; Set a larger maximum upload size\nupload_max_filesize=${UPLOAD_MAX_FILESIZE}\npost_max_size=${UPLOAD_MAX_FILESIZE}\n\n; Write error log to syslog for easier debugging\nerror_log=syslog\n\n; Performance optimizations\nopcache.enable=1\nopcache.memory_consumption=128\nopcache.interned_strings_buffer=8\nopcache.max_accelerated_files=10000\nopcache.revalidate_freq=2\nopcache.save_comments=1\nPHPCONF\n        print_success \"PHP configuration overrides created\"\n    else\n        print_info \"PHP configuration overrides already exist\"\n    fi\n\n    # Update PHP-FPM pool configuration for dynamic process management\n    if [[ -f \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\" ]]; then\n        print_step \"Updating PHP-FPM pool configuration...\"\n\n        # Backup original config\n        if [[ ! -f \"${PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF}.original\" ]]; then\n            cp \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\" \"${PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF}.original\"\n        fi\n\n        # Update pm settings for dynamic process management\n        sed -i \"s/^pm = .*/pm = dynamic/\" \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\"\n        sed -i \"s/^pm.max_children = .*/pm.max_children = ${MAX_PHP_PROCESSES}/\" \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\"\n        sed -i \"s/^pm.start_servers = .*/pm.start_servers = 5/\" \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\"\n        sed -i \"s/^pm.min_spare_servers = .*/pm.min_spare_servers = 2/\" \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\"\n        sed -i \"s/^pm.max_spare_servers = .*/pm.max_spare_servers = 10/\" \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\"\n\n        # Restart PHP-FPM to apply changes\n        print_step \"Restarting PHP-FPM...\"\n        systemctl restart \"php${PHP_VERSION}-fpm\"\n        print_success \"PHP-FPM configuration optimized\"\n    else\n        print_warning \"PHP-FPM pool configuration not found\"\n    fi\n}\n\nget_php_fpm_socket() {\n    # Find the PHP-FPM socket path dynamically\n    PHP_VERSION=$(php -r \"echo PHP_MAJOR_VERSION.'.'.PHP_MINOR_VERSION;\")\n    PHP_FPM_SOCKET=\"/run/php/php${PHP_VERSION}-fpm.sock\"\n\n    if [[ ! -S \"$PHP_FPM_SOCKET\" ]]; then\n        # Try to find any PHP-FPM socket\n        PHP_FPM_SOCKET=$(find /run/php -name \"php*-fpm.sock\" 2>/dev/null | head -1)\n    fi\n\n    echo \"$PHP_FPM_SOCKET\"\n}\n\nconfigure_gzip_compression() {\n    print_step \"Configuring gzip compression...\"\n\n    # Create gzip configuration file if it doesn't exist\n    if [[ ! -f \"${NGINX_CONF_DIR}/conf.d/gzip.conf\" ]]; then\n        cat > \"${NGINX_CONF_DIR}/conf.d/gzip.conf\" << 'GZIPCONF'\n# Gzip compression configuration\n# Credit: https://github.com/h5bp/server-configs-nginx/\n\n# Enable gzip compression\ngzip on;\n\n# Compression level (1-9)\n# 6 is a good compromise between size and CPU usage, offering about 75%\n# reduction for most ASCII files\ngzip_comp_level 6;\n\n# Don't compress anything that's already small\ngzip_min_length 256;\n\n# Compress data even for clients connecting via proxies\ngzip_proxied any;\n\n# Tell proxies to cache both gzipped and regular versions\ngzip_vary on;\n\n# Compress these MIME types (text/html is always compressed)\ngzip_types\n \"${AVAIL_MEM_BYTES}/${PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES}+5\" | bc 2>/dev/null || echo \"10\")\n\n    # Cap at reasonable maximum\n    if [[ \"$MAX_PHP_PROCESSES\" -gt 50 ]]; then\n        MAX_PHP_PROCESSES=50\n optimizations\nopcache.enable=1\nopcache.memory_consumption=128\nopcache.interned_strings_buffer=8\nopcache.max_accelerated_files=10000\nopcache.revalidate_freq=2\nopcache.save_comments=1\nPHPCONF\n        print_success \"PHP configuration overrides created\"\n    else\n        print_info \"PHP configuration overrides already exist\"\n    fi\n\n    # Update PHP-FPM pool configuration for dynamic process management\n    if [[ -f \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\" ]]; then\n        print_step \"Updating PHP-FPM pool configuration...\"\n\n        # Backup original config\n        if [[ ! -f \"${PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF}.original\" ]]; then\n            cp \"$PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF\" \"${PHP_FPM_POOL_CONF}.original\"\n        fi\n\n        # Update pm settings for dynamic process management\n fi\n}\n\nget_php_fpm_socket() {\n    # Find the PHP-FPM socket path dynamically\n    PHP_VERSION=$(php -r \"echo PHP_MAJOR_VERSION.'.'.PHP_MINOR_VERSION;\")\n    PHP_FPM_SOCKET=\"/run/php/php${PHP_VERSION}-fpm.sock\"\n\n    if [[ ! -S \"$PHP_FPM_SOCKET\" ]]; then\n        # Try to find any PHP-FPM socket\n        PHP_FPM_SOCKET=$(find /run/php -name Handle -1 (unlimited) as a special case, using 256M default\n# 2. Validate that converted values are positive integers\n# 3. Use integer arithmetic instead of bc for the calculation\n# 4. Ensure result is always between 5 and 50\n#===============================================================================\n\n# Color definitions\nRED='\\033[0;31m'\nGREEN='\\033[0;32m'\nYELLOW='\\033[1;33m'\nCYAN='\\033[0;36m'\nNC='\\033[0m'\n\necho -e \"${CYAN}=== Testing PHP Memory Limit Parsing Fix ===${NC}\"\necho -e \"${CYAN}Issue: https://github.com/andchir/install_scripts/issues/123${NC}\"\necho \"\"\n\n# Simulate available memory (6474 MB = 6474 * 1024 KB, as reported in the issue)\nAVAIL_MEM=6631424  # in KB (approximately 6474 MB)\nAVAIL_MEM_BYTES=$((AVAIL_MEM * 1024))\n\necho \"Simulating server with $((AVAIL_MEM / 1024)) MB available memory\"\necho \"\"\n\n# Test the fixed calculation function\ntest_fixed_calculation() {\n    local PHP_MEM_LIMIT=\"$1\"\n    local PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES\n\n    # Handle special case when memory_limit is -1 (unlimited)\n    if [[ \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT\" == \"-1\" ]]; then\n            PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=$(echo \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT\" | numfmt --from=iec 2>/dev/null || echo \"\")\n        else\n            # Fallback manual conversion for common formats (for testing without numfmt)\n            case \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT\" in\n                *M) PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=$((${PHP_MEM_LIMIT%M} * 1024 * 1024)) ;;\n                *G) PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=$((${PHP_MEM_LIMIT%G} * 1024 * 1024 * 1024)) ;;\n                *K) PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=$((${PHP_MEM_LIMIT%K} * 1024)) ;;\n                [0-9]*) PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=$PHP_MEM_LIMIT ;;\n                *) PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=\"\" ;;\n            esac\n        fi\n\n        # Validate the result is a positive number\n        if [[ -z \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES\" ]] || ! [[ \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES\" =~ ^[0-9]+$ ]] || [[ \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES\" -le 0 ]]; then\n            PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=134217728\n            echo \"  → Invalid value, using default 128M (134217728 bytes)\"\n        else\n            echo \"  → Converted to $PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES bytes\"\n        fi\n    fi\n\n    # Calculate max processes using integer arithmetic (avoids bc dependency)\n    local MAX_PHP_PROCESSES=$((AVAIL_MEM_BYTES / PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES))\n\n    # Ensure minimum of 5 processes\n    if [[ \"$MAX_PHP_PROCESSES\" -lt 5 ]]; then\n        MAX_PHP_PROCESSES=5\n    fi\n\n    # Cap at reasonable maximum of 50\n    if [[ \"$MAX_PHP_PROCESSES\" -gt 50 ]]; then\n        MAX_PHP_PROCESSES=50\n    fi\n\n    echo \"  → MAX_PHP_PROCESSES: $MAX_PHP_PROCESSES\"\n\n    # Validate result is sensible (not negative, within bounds)\n    if [[ \"$MAX_PHP_PROCESSES\" -ge 5 ]] && [[ \"$MAX_PHP_PROCESSES\" -le 50 ]]; Деление доступной памяти на отрицательное число даёт отрицательный результат\n3. Handle -1 (unlimited) as a special case, using 256M default\n+# 2. Validate that converted values are positive integers\n+# 3. Use integer arithmetic instead of bc for the calculation\n+# 4. Ensure result is always between 5 and 50\n+#===============================================================================\n+\n+# Color definitions\n+RED='\\033[0;31m'\n+GREEN='\\033[0;32m'\n+YELLOW='\\033[1;33m'\n+CYAN='\\033[0;36m'\n+NC='\\033[0m'\n+\n+echo -e \"${CYAN}=== Testing PHP Memory Limit Parsing Fix ===${NC}\"\n+echo -e \"${CYAN}Issue: https://github.com/andchir/install_scripts/issues/123${NC}\"\n+echo \"\"\n+\n+# Simulate available memory (6474 MB = 6474 * 1024 KB, as reported in the issue)\n+AVAIL_MEM=6631424  # in KB (approximately 6474 MB)\n+AVAIL_MEM_BYTES=$((AVAIL_MEM * 1024))\n+\n+echo \"Simulating server with $((AVAIL_MEM / 1024)) MB available memory\"\n+echo \"\"\n+\n+# Test the fixed calculation function\n+test_fixed_calculation() {\n+    local PHP_MEM_LIMIT=\"$1\"\n+    local PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES\n+\n+    # Handle special case when memory_limit is -1 (unlimited)\n+    if [[ \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT\" == \"-1\" ]]; then\n+        PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=268435456\n+        echo \"  → Unlimited (-1) detected, using 256M (268435456 bytes)\"\n+    elif [[ -z \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT\" ]] || [[ \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT\" == \"0\" ]]; then\n+        PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=134217728\n+        echo \"  → Empty/zero value, using default 128M (134217728 bytes)\"\n+    else\n+        # Try to convert using numfmt if available\n+        if command -v numfmt &> /dev/null; then\n+            PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=$(echo \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT\" | numfmt --from=iec 2>/dev/null || echo \"\")\n+        else\n+            # Fallback manual conversion for common formats (for testing without numfmt)\n+            case \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT\" in\n+                *M) PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=$((${PHP_MEM_LIMIT%M} * 1024 * 1024)) ;;\n+                *G) PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=$((${PHP_MEM_LIMIT%G} * 1024 * 1024 * 1024)) ;;\n+                *K) PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=$((${PHP_MEM_LIMIT%K} * 1024)) ;;\n+                [0-9]*) PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=$PHP_MEM_LIMIT ;;\n+                *) PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES=\"\" ;;\n+            esac\n+        fi\n+\n+        # Validate the result is a positive number\n+        if [[ -z \"$PHP_MEM_LIMIT_BYTES\" ]] || !         "type": "text",
        "text": "## Summary\n\nI've successfully fixed the WordPress installation script issue reported in [#123](https://github.com/andchir/install_scripts/issues/123).\n\n### Problem\nWhen PHP `memory_limit` is set to `-1` (unlimited), the `optimize_php_fpm` function calculated a negative value for `pm.max_children` (-6789435387), causing PHP-FPM to fail with:\n```\nERROR: unable to allocate 2102983071568 bytes in shared memory\nERROR: FPM initialization failed\n```\n\n### Root Cause\n1. `numfmt --from=iec` cannot parse `-1` and fails silently\n2. Division of available memory by `-1` or an invalid value produces a large negative number\n3. This negative value was used directly as `pm.max_children` in PHP-FPM configuration\n\n### Solution (in `scripts/wordpress.sh:619-670`)\n- Added explicit handling for `memory_limit = -1` (unlimited) → uses 256M as default\n- Added handling for empty or zero values → uses 128M as default\n- Added validation that the converted value is a positive integer\n- Replaced `bc` with bash integer arithmetic to avoid dependency issues\n- Ensured result is always clamped between 5 and 50 processes\n\n### Testing\nAdded `experiments/test_php_memory_limit_parsing.sh` that validates all edge cases:\n- `-1` (unlimited) → 25 processes (for 6.5GB memory)\n- Valid values (`128M`, `256M`, `512M`, `1G`) → correct calculation\n- Invalid values (`0`, empty, `invalid`) → falls back to 128M\n\n### Pull Request\n- **URL**: https://github.com/andchir/install_scripts/pull/124\n- **Status**: Ready for review\n- **Fixes**: Issue #123"
